puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	then pierce the fat completely with water about half an inch thick, and remove all the water, then put your fingers in, and keep the fat on top; but don't touch the chest bone, but only the fat; cut all around or piece by piece along his side carefully, for if you don't do it carefully, water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the egg jumps to your work, you must reset it in its place when you have completed the task of hatching; then unite the two sides from the knee down to one seam, then treat it as you would other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit. de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	from the birth of the child that comes out with one hand during
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to engineer in order to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If one cannot bring it back, then make her stand up and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she can't walk, I make her lie on a bed, and I straighten her legs outwards;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then follow the massage that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she doesn't give birth, make her sit on a chair, then try to guide the hand back;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and direct the birth according to natural position, make her sneeze, and command her to push until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the exit of the child from its neck, and spread out its hands, and its face turned towards its mother's back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary to strike his hand with a stick gently, then turn it little by little, and lead him gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when he is even, place on the natural movement of elevation and oil, as we have said, then command him to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	And once you've done this, make her sit on a stool, and command her to pray; and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In this same manner for all the second part
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to doing this in this way for the entire second part, if you have the second part up to your nail, until all the moisture is drained;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	And if it descends below its place on its face and neck, if you start from the navel, do not let it be held back, and let the child die;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then guide the child inside, until you place it as it should be, and command the woman not to give any contractions at all:
adonques si istra legierement.	Therefore, if you gently treat it.
de l’issue des gemelz	Regarding the delivery of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are often born, and sometimes three or even four at a time; this is not an uncommon occurrence, it just happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are extraordinary things, and do not live long, if they do appear.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know this, for they multiply, and are removed by the scab that afflicts them, which is bound to the sweat.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And they also come out naturally like all under them, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they come out painfully, with the cure as we have said, and if it is a subtle ailment, then do what she does immediately and lightly.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And do so in such a way that it benefits the health.
de plusors enfans	Of several children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	None are formed in marriage. Either once or twice or three times or four times or five times or six times or seven times, and they are all formed like an infant according to the measurement of their glory,
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	and it is necessary that the maid know about everything such as this, for by chance she might come across something similar.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	do it according to what is proper.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman who has lost her dead child or is carrying it inside, as I explained in the section on division, if it does not come out, and you are forced to operate with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary that you know whether the woman is in good health, and if she has not experienced any accidents or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary that the woman be supported on her back, and have her hands placed under her chin, and her legs lifted;
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And let the minister apply a piece of wax of two inches, or bind it to the bed so that it does not burn during childbirth;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the pregnant woman with oily camphor and mixtures of sweet fennel and linseed, then smear her hands with these oils and these camphors.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	Then support the pregnant woman lightly, then let her give birth in one hour or as much time as it takes for the pains to be manageable.
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and take care that when the child appears, it descends onto its head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	If the tumors are planted in his eyes or at his neck or in his mouth or under his palate or near his beard or on the forehead or close to the ribs,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if it descends from the joints, then it's implanted or gripped and in the middle of the ribs;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	It is necessary that you cut the tumor with your right hand and place the curve between the fingers of your left hand, and push it lightly with all your hand, and implant the tumor in none of these places which we have said, until it reaches the hollow thing.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the form of the tumor:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then find a third person or another surgeon, if necessary, so that the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then move them equally on one side and the other, so that they can be used, and make the surgeons' teeth capable of holding them, as shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if a part remains, if any of its duties is oiled, and grease them in that part, and draw the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if nothing remains, place this piece of bone or higher up, and do this until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be brought back by squeezing,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap with a single bandage until it exits completely;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then apply the compress at the joint of the foot or on the leg, and similarly you should do this with the other hand, and with both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child's head is large and it is tilted in the birth canal, or if its nose is assembled with its chin,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	If it is necessary for you to pinch the sharp sputum between your fingers, and make the head and remove the water;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you will find it at the tool that is called "almidach", from which the form comes with tools or chapters after this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and in the same manner make so that their heads grow naturally to a great size;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	then pull out the bones with tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	And if the shoulder joint jumps and it is held by force, then it will be split as long as the moisture is or worse originates from;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot escape, cut it piece by piece until you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or around the sides, you must puncture it as far as the moisture goes.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if it appears in his feet, it is a light condition, and its extension to the mouth of the womb is also light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it's protruding at the belly or on the breast, it should be extracted with one and a half feet of wrapping around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and when the belly or the breast is affected by moisture as long as that moisture is present.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if another bone is involved and the head of the shoulder remains displaced,
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if he has difficulty getting his hand through the socket, and leads it until it reaches the opening of the socket;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then I add a spoonful or two, and stir it;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the sore is narrowed due to an abscess that has come there, it should not be worked on,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	otherwise, it's best to apply moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the treatment involves plastering, and if possible, use waters that are softening and moisturizing.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the fetus is within its mother's body, and you can place it evenly, follow what we've instructed regarding live childbirth;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if unable to do so whole, split the mother through her parts, and don't leave any remnants of the fetus.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And once you have done this, follow what we've instructed about incisions when dealing with pus-filled abscesses that occur in the groin area;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if bleeding occurs, then apply hot water to restrict it, and proceed with other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman who had given birth to one child, then she gave birth to another near that one, and the second also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, there was an abscess in her womb, and it grew so much that she opened [it], and started experiencing severe pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned for treatment, and I thought for a long time, and could not find the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied strong plaster to it, and out came a bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because a person's belly has no bone.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I looked for the wound, and I searched with my hands through the flesh until the woman felt better;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And I attended to the woman long after that, and at this point there was a slight improvement in her condition;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have recorded this chapter merely for when, should a master find an unfamiliar thing, he knows how to offer aid.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to reset the dislocated joint to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Next comes the form of the pressure method, which is described in these books; and for each two turns use each of two arms with each of two fingers.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Always, let the horns be finer than the restrainer, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And let the mouth be of wood, two spans wide, and the border of the trees one span, and a long half palm;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in between the two beams be two spans of this same wood, which should be firm on both sides, a half palm long or slightly more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two braces are set in the mouth of the mortar so that they can be opened when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, similar yet more delicate and lighter, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the shape of the pliers.
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	And you need two shoulders, say two adjustments, just like what you see, one of the length of a hand, and two fingers in width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	And when you see the opening of the artery with all the instrument, make the woman sit on one bed, her knees hanging and her legs spread apart,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	Then fasten the two adjustments together on the artery, and hold the handle of the instrument between her buttocks;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with the entire instrument, just like you would with equal forceps, according to the amount that you see opening the mouth of the artery, until the operation completes what she desires.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	This instrument is entirely raised and multiplied according to its resemblance; and when you have prepared them, the work progresses faster, and they are higher for men in terms of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not despair over the instrument but prepare it, because its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second stage of labor is retained during birth, you must instruct the mother to hold back her urine, and then make her breathe out through the nose, and keep your hands on her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she does this by jumping, it's well done.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not this way, take two pots, and make a lid or cover for each, then put in herbs that can open the mouth of the wound, like alum, rue, anise, chamomile, laurel leaves and mint.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or none of them, should be cooked or boiled in water on the fire; then put a reed or a cover inside each pot, and place one head in the wound.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Let the steam rise within the wound until it begins to evaporate; then make it exhale, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If you jump to the next one immediately.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not cured, one instructs the patient to moisten her left hand with sesame oil or with myrrh, and then apply the paste in its natural state,
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And seeks the second; and when she finds it, if she retrieves and gradually extends it slightly, so that no part of the joint is involved in the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But it must be gently moved to the right and left, and then pulled; if this is done, it will come out and become loose.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if there is tightness in the throat's muscles, we have spoken of the treatment for coughing and herb fumigation;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not involve anything that we have discussed, then be sure not to force it during treatment.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary for the person at the throat of the mare to tie them to the woman's mouth, then apply ointment from Tetrafarmacopeia and enemas.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if it is purged, then strength will return; but still, if she recovers and yet there's an unpleasant smell in the stomach and head, and irritates the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Then indeed, suitable fumigations are necessary for this: none of the old ones have proven effective fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the tool with which one fumigates a woman during labor and delivery is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it resembles in appearance to a cane, and one places the narrow part of it in the natural opening, and the heads broadly upon the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let there be the fumigations above the coals, and the tree until it is spent, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	To pierce the base
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	There are infants born who do not have the base pierced, but rather, they possess a subtle secret:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	So it is necessary for the midwife to pierce this secret according to its place, and do not prick it with an excessively sharp needle, and preserve the wound so that it does not touch;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place on wet wool in wine and oil, then apply the salve until the skin heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt whether it will stay in place, then apply or insert a hazel rod, and leave the patient's hands bound for several days, and remove the rod when the child wishes to move about.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And it is not sudden scarring of wounds or abscesses that comes; if you need to treat the scarring, you should do this: if you must cure it, as we have said regarding the hazel rod.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the瘘管 from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that originate from underneath are called nodes, and those that come from above the foundation or in the space between two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is one or more fistulas; and when that node is old, it works, and produces moisture which appears white or subtle bows,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and these fistulas are Persian; and they are known by the fact that there is expulsion or wind when the patient expels, and sometimes in moving one direction.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that extend up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis; and they reach up to the joint of the leg, and up to the root of the testicles.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula is present at the foundation, and not present:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should strike your index finger or the foundation, and insert a fine needle or an arachnid or iron pin into the fistula when there is no winding.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has winding, then you should insert a fine tentacle, or one of a horse's hair, as long as you feel the tentacle or the hair at your index finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge or windiness nor worms, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not puncture at all; if you hasten to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is long up to the bladder or even where urine is conducted, if it jumps with urine, and cannot be sealed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it penetrates up to the knee joint, then the veins run up to the top;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twisting and if there's an intense pain inside, then it will remain as such until it heals on its own, and it doesn't respond to medicine or ointment treatment.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And with these Persian fistulas, there is no use of strength nor the vain intervention of those who meddle in such affairs.

des plaies	of wounds

et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not place anything cold on the wound, for the substance of the neck is cold, and its continuity goes with the brain which is the highest limb.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but use warm medicine instead, such as rose water rinsed with gentle water, and mixed with rose oil, and also clean cumin rinsed in gentle water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones of the body according to this manner, and moist applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then treat it so that it heals properly.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and filled with blood, then pierce or lower further;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and blood starts flowing out, then open it up, and let it bleed, and if needed, remove it and properly cauterize.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if he cuts the neck or the knees, and the path is kept clear, so that the meat goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if he cuts the knee above the neck and does not touch the neck but resets it according to its natural form;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then stretch it, and let it heal for some days, then treat with ointments that dry out until it is clean;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if it causes an impression on the bone, then you must take action;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are fragments of bone, remove them thoroughly if you can,
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let it be drained and cleaned out.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a瘘管, then the treatment should be as I have said in my chapter on this subject.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	From the wound of a spear or a knife.
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's from a spear or a knife wound, and the wound is deep, examine if there is any suction in the wound: you will then know that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it isn't deep and the blood is still flowing freely throughout, do not apply any powder or bind it up in the first hour unless the blood stops flowing completely.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And arouses at the heart, and occupies the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive balm, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have a balm, put old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and make the patient rest on the wound for three days, or four, or more if necessary;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	If there is no spasm, nor unpleasant heart tremors, nor sudden movements due to pain;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see the good conditions, if you know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it with remedies and other treatments, while keeping it clean;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	And if it cannot heal properly, and there is an incision or wound, then you will know that there is a fistula; treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is a result of an incision from a sword or knife, and it is simple, or worse, or behind, if the treatment for him who is in front;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it's large, sew it up; and if it's small, use powder, and if it's pressed into the bone, and cut parts out of it, then treat the wound, and remove any foreign debris if they are exposed;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not exposed, let the wound fester, aiding in the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other members is judgment made as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	about the rupture of the stomach
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the stomach are large, medium-sized, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound, it jumps once the intestine, or the nerves of the intestines, causing an invasion by them;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And healing is more difficult, and there is no time better than a small wound compared to large ones.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one should not put the intestines in again immediately; instead, they should be inserted little by little.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	Because when the intestines swell up as soon as they feel cold, if you insert them further in,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because of this, it's better to perform surgery on the smaller wound, for this reason you should insert the intestines to their original position along with others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the tearing of the belly follows four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common stitches occur in the stitch of the belly,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the stitches for other wounds on the body and two other types of stitches are common to other injuries;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	yet they are more appropriate with the stitch in the belly, and I will describe each one separately.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and there's no part of the intestine involved,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and when it comes to putting things back, this can be done through either of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when he's cold, warm him this way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Wet a cloth or use one millilitre of water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in water that is infused and contains cypress and thorns,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and let the intestines cook until they are so full they cannot be squeezed out;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this has been done by restraining the wine intake, and made it stop causing swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling depart, if season with water or broth or whatever cooked vegetables there are,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because thus does the intake become limited to little things;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they make a bit more of the incision with the instrument used for extracting thorns;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to let the wound grow,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	which we should not cut without great necessity, nor at random;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and these are the tools to split them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside at the bend and not outward, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound has grown larger, and the intestines have escaped,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if he resets it according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	should you have the ability, because this is what matters.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is broad and it's located on the abdominal area,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	It is necessary for you to make the patient feel comfortable on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and place their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if she is in the abdominal region,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	and put her head and buttocks higher than the abdominal parts,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	And similarly if there is a rupture due to wind in one of the two parts of the abdomen.
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	if you understand that the part that has shrunk should be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus it is appropriate to administer what I say about large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what you are equipped with,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have in your hands one, a surgeon who cuts through the entire tear with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	and bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of stitches,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	And it is that you take one needle or several, according to the amount of width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave at the edge of the wound, that is one inch in size, and I place a needle or where it has one good strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two sides of the skin with the two sides of the artery.
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is within the skin, until you pierce it from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	And gather the two main parts of the siphon along with three others together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	and stretch a doubled thread around the needle for two inches,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then join the two edges of the wound with an addition,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave one inch of space, and insert another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then with the thread just as you made the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and keep doing this according to what you need for the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is contained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and that the needles are balanced between fine and thick ones,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	For the fine needles cut all the flesh, and the too large ones can't enter properly:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Therefore, they should be smaller;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it's not good to have the needles sticking too far out from the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	They should not cut or widen the wound before sewing it up;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cover the punctures of the needles so they do not irritate the patient during sleep,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and set up tents or cloths over the puncture areas from the needles to keep them clean and prevent infection.
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this way of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	For there was a pricking sensation at two points.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it involves sewing together the two strips of leather and two strips of skin into one needle with half a strong thread;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced all four pieces together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	if you reinsert the needle at the part where you started, in the way one stitches with threads;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a space between each stitch as large as a minor do;
ceste costure sevent li home,	these stitches form the seam,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew up a wound made by one's hand, or belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was without a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and had a wound larger than a palm's width,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and contained intestines as long as two palms,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in the middle of the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine to its place once it had been out for twenty-one hours,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound healed up until fifteen days, and I treated it, and it was sound.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they believed that he would die, and this was a wonder;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not treat him with ointment, for I was in one region where none could be found, nor any medicines;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And change the cloth covering the wound twice a day, and wash it with honey water until it is clean.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Or I will tell you the two proper methods of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and thread it starting from the outside part until inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	Once it has pierced straight through in line, leave the thread attached to where you have inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	And make another piercing from inside of the other part up to this one outside;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this seam is that you sew it in the same way as the leatherworker fleshes the skins,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and leave once the seam on one side, and take it on another, until the entire seam is completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second way of sewing, as Galen stated properly,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	It's thus like what some do, who unite the two parts naturally together,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and press one of the ends of the syringe against the other end, in such manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stick a needle or a piece of thread near the gallbladder area, and make it pierce only that side.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and let the two ends of the needle hang;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle, and make it pierce from the outer part until inside.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	for the two shoulders of the socket;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both from the outer part until inside, in two other shoulders of the scapula that are opposite each other;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the usual and common way of sewing.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen stated this word and no one denies it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	We must stitch the belly with two needles, where there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one should stab one needle from one side and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew bullet wounds;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the rupture occurs within the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	then the stitch is more dangerous than in other cases of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is such as the judgment of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it follows that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood, just as the art has made it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	If set back in the intestine, and at the cut; then put on the powder that causes swelling,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if it has been defecated, then apply no ointment until the wound heals,
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and sew the thread, and stitch up the skin, and heal the wound;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as usual until it heals;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you don't have medicines, place it up, as soon as it starts to bleed, old cotton,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And shake it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	But you don't need other medicines in various preparations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	And if you doubt that the wound might affect the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	If you need to moisten with light oil heated to body temperature, or in oil that is lightly roasting,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and apply it inside the joints, and over the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if you feel pain or gangrene in the bowels, and this occurs many times,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if you use black wine enemas, and especially if gangrene reaches up to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And penetrate within, and know that when it is large intestine, it is lighter to heal than the smaller ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine which they call "small" cannot be healed if it is wounded,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And this is due to the disposition of the veins that are there, and by the subtlety of the whole body, and its approach to its own nature with nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if pus escapes from the wound, it is treated in the same way as if it were intestine when it's still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and turned red or black, then you should tie the part that is black, so that no bleeding occurs there.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligament,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place both ends of it down from the part above the wound until below for to ease extraction when the roots pull out, and the wound heals.
de la routure dou boueil	Of the breach of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are involved, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in any way,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that a man was pierced by or through his abdomen with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	And the wound was located on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And it became infected and formed a fistula, causing both malabsorption and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it according to what I could do, and kept refining the treatment until it healed, and bound the edges.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw that it was healing, I wondered if there might be disease in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And there was no harm, but it stayed in better positions, eating and drinking.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And some experimenters say that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be treated in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large eggs, then join the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	And when the mouth of the patient has been opened, place it between the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if its mouth is stretched upwards;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then support its head, and this position should be such that it cannot release it.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then place another wriggle in the same way as before, until the wound is fully treated;
et cout la plaie.	And thus the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the food heats up inside, and does not cause any harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And one can tie the intestine with a fine thread cut from an animal's intestine,
en teil maniere:	"By this method:"
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	Take hold of this thread from the intestines where it is slightly burned,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie firmly to this end of the thread that is one inch in length, a fine linen thread twisted together.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then sew the thread into the needle and stitch it through the intestines, and correct the dislocation;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this way of stitching without any cuts is only according to the path of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is big and wide, especially when it's in one of the intestinal chambers, if there is no organ or health there, due to subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from a fistula or where it might be.
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that any wound or abscess, as it matures, is universally called "fistula".
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And likewise when she is hairy and returns to her origin.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the yellowish hardened and whitish nodulation, where no pain is felt.
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it is also covered like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes in clear white, and other times in thick substance;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes it is scarce, and other times sufficient.
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken about it in the division of wounds, that every wound which is not healed, and there's no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	This can only be due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	That is to say, it's due to the weakness or obstruction in the blood or wound;
ou por sa malice;	or because of its malevolence;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	because there is hard flesh within, and above the lips, which does not allow hair to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	there is too much fat;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	the veins are swollen, and the matter is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good for treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	because the corruption is like a pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	because the properties in the region are late for digestion, and the health process is slow, escaping naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have shown all these causes, and the signs, and the remedies for medicines in this division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	It is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of fistulas which is done through manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas can occur in all limbs, both internal and external;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that originate from the large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the stomach, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	At the spinal column of the back, or at any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And if it comes to the property of the main member, and to their similar characteristics.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the ulcers that are like this are difficult to heal, and there is nothing else but hard work, and lack of knowledge;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is no ulcer that does not reach up to the one I have said, and you will be able to complete the treatment,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And you will learn to recognize it, if you take a spider's web or a metal thread, if the duct is straight, then choose;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the duct is bent, seek out a delicate fishing line;
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because when fishing the fish twists and moves in the bends;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the duct is hard to find even with spider webs or metal threads,

et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient to clearly describe the pain they feel when you press their hand, and the location of the pain;

et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is deeply and correctly placed, it must be sealed from below upwards, as much as you can.
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then place wet cloths in medicinal water, and fill them until they reach the tip of the fistula.

et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then apply healing ointments for a long time until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	And if it cannot be treated by this method, then apply heat treatment as we have described.
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is decayed due to the ulceration, then operate on it.

et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not healthy, and you must use them as before.
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	Know that you are not yet done until this point:

Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was a young man of about thirty years old, who had a pain in his leg due to something that came from within the body,
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	As long as the contents reached the leg, and was drained of a large abscess, and there was no reason to open it;

mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not do so until I copied within half of the bone, and I laid it out to all its size,

Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	But because of frequent blood loss, he was completely healed,
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And there emerged from within the bone a hard flesh, and it was well arranged and had no harm or opposite effect at all in every way, neither outward nor inward.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, such that it should be treated in this manner:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	take one string, and draw it tight at the end of the bone that is exposed,
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	and command none to extend it upwards;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	And take one more thread of wool larger than the first tie, and tie it above the skin which is around the bone,

et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	and place one piece of charcoal or a board under the bone to cover the rotten flesh;

si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	if you consider the tool that suits your needs according to what is appropriate.
dou feu	The fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The shoulder dislocates either due to a blow inside, or due to a fall;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	and when you have treated that burn with the application of medicines, and if they do not benefit at all,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	then it is necessary to cover that limb up to where the burn comes,
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	if indeed the patient escapes through death, or by evil intent, which is greater than the fault of the limb;
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	and the signs are that the limbs turn black, as if they have been burnt by fire,
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	and after the blackness, comes the corrosion spreading from limb to limb,
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	and spreads throughout the body; if you delay with copper treatment,
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	And if it's due to striking with some venomous sea animals, such as the scorpion of the sea and snake-like creatures,
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	If the corrosion is on the head near the nose, if you cut it, and do not give it space to come up to the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it comes up to the hand, if you cut at the joint, so that the corrosion does not spread up to the elbow;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	And if it comes to the arm, you cut it; and if it passes the knife, then it is death.
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	and it would be wise only beyond what its effectiveness allows.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	and do the same until the corrosion reaches or the plate: if it reaches at the first joint, then cut after the other joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	and if it comes to the plate, then cut all of the plate.
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	And if it ascends to the leg, then it is at the knee joint;
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	And if it comes over the knee, there's no other issue than to let the patient die;

puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part .i. drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain,	then place or sew it with silk, and put one strip of linen from each side, so that the silk does not touch the healthy bone;
et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	and let the patient undergo another injury and abscess.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment,	And when bleeding occurs during this process, quickly cauterize the wound,
ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans; puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie,	In the first step, you apply certain powder restraining substances; then return to your medicine until its completion,
puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then bind the injured limb with a reliable bandage, and treat it until it heals properly;
et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	and I will tell you what happened in one of those homes:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	he experienced a darkness that seemed like the presence of fire,
et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	And this corrosion came first on his second toe, until it consumed all of the toe;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	And when the injury encounters the corrosion, it seeks to cover the foot, and becomes healthy;

car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	for the power of the ome was weak; and he completely lost hope, returned to his land,

et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	And I have written this merely for those who may need to perform it otherwise, if required.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	No abscess forms within the fatty layer of the flesh, and remains so long as it causes a large gathering of pus;
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	And then spreads and perforates, and pus jumps at the pus, and remains in the veins, as if they were vessels;
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	And the skin above is also as thin as a single piece of silk,
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	And do not extend until to the bone, or to the nerve, and such diseases are called "safe",
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	and is not called "fistula";
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	but if it extends so much that it reaches up to the bone on all sides, then it is called "fistula";

Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	And if you have found that the skin is burning, and corruption isn't fully present,
et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	and if the skin is thick with pus, then cleanse it with a collyrium like this:

adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	Therefore use an Egyptian enema made as follows:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	Take it easily, and oil, and litharge, equally, and cook them together in a single pot over the fire,

et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres,	And if the patient cannot bear it, neither can Egyptian remedies nor ash water help.
si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	if they use a solution of water and honey or has a little lye in it;

de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of cutting out the pus from the nail.

la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	The pain of the numbness in the hand

Des vils	Of the lowly
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	Here come swollen veins packed tightly, filled with surplus melancholic substances, that cause afflictions in various parts of the body;
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	And it happens more often in legs of those who walk on foot and work, than in others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	Therefore, you should give them an emetic for the bile once, and then treat it with basilisk afterwards.
Li cure de fer si est selonc .ij. manieres: l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	The iron treatment can be done in two ways: one is to apply the paste and bleed them of black blood;

Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere: arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez,	The method for this is as follows: first raise the hot leg water quite forcefully, until the large vein becomes delicate.

De la voinne civile	From the civil vein
Ceste voinne est enjanree en jambes, en chaudes parties ou il ne naist herbes ne arbre, et en terre ou il n’a point de moistor;	This vein is found in the legs, in warm parts where no herbs or trees grow, and in the ground that has no moisture.

Des vers qui naissent entre cuir et char	Worms that emerge between skin and muscle
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «maladie de buef», por ceu qu’elle avient maintes fois as bués,	This disease is called in our land "cattle disease", because it often affects cattle,
et est un petis vers qui naist entre cuir et char, et va par tout le cors montant et dessendant,	And there is a small worm that emerges between skin and muscle, and travels throughout the body going up and down,
et le sent om bien a l’aler de membre en membre, tant qu’il desront le cuir ou il vait, et saut fuer;	And one feels it well in each limb upon its ascent, until it reaches the skin where it was going, and jumps forth;
et est enjanrez de porriture d’aucunes humors, si com vienent vers et serpens et lumbris et ascarides ou ventre;	And it is bound up with corruption of certain fluids, such as worms and snakes and roundworms or in the stomach;
et doute on de son malice, car quant il va par le cors, et il monte au chief, et il vient a l’oil,	And there is doubt about its nature, for when it travels through the body, and rises to the head, and comes to the eye,
par aventure rentre, et destruit l’oil; et ceu avient maintes fois.	By chance it enters and destroys the eye; and this happens many times.
Quant tu le vues curer et traire, si ne puet on fuers que quant il vait:	When you see it being treated and drained, one can only do so until it's almost over:
si covient donques que tu lies le leu desus et desoz d’un fort liien bien estroitement,	Therefore, it is necessary that you tie the wound above and below with a strong ligature tightly,
puis cope sus et le trai fuer, et se li vers est em parfont en la char, et tu ne le trueves,	Then cut upwards and drain it, and if it goes deep into the flesh, you won't find it,
si le cauterize de feu sus, tant qu’il muire;	If you heat the cautery,
et li plus grans nuisemens que il fait, si est qu’il corront l’oil, si com nos avons dit;	and the greater injuries that it causes, if they flow in the eye, as we have said;
et se tu le vois venir ou chief pres de l’oil, si estraint desoz lui le sorcil forment, puis cope sus, et le trai fuer;	and when you see it coming near to or close to the eye, if you cover him with your hand in front of it, then move upwards, and push it firmly;
et covient user le malaide de mundifiement de cors de medicines solutives por les males humors porries,	and it is necessary to use the patient for the purification of bodily humors by medicines that dissolve, in order to treat illnesses caused by them,
et se warse de viandes enjanrans porriture.	And if it comes to cooking meat causing putrefaction.
De la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	Of the pain that comes from wind disturbances
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «vakirir», et est une dolor que vient en aucuns membres,	This illness is called "vakirir" in our land, and it is a pain that affects some parts of the body,
et pues se mue de membre en membre; et je vis ceu que je vos di.	And it travels from limb to limb; and I have seen what I am telling you.
Je fui apelez a une femme malaide, et me descovrit som bras, et vis une petite enfleure en la voinne dou brais;	I was summoned to tend a woman in labor, and she showed me her arms, revealing a small swelling in the vein beneath them;
et .i. poc aprés, li vis monter ausi com un ver a l’espaule,	And soon after, I noticed it rise as if a worm was moving up to her shoulder,
plus tost que nulle chose, ausi com vif argent quant il cort de leu a autre;	Quicker than anything else, like quicksilver when it is cut from one place to another;
li dolor se departit de celui leu, et se ficha en l’espaule,	The pain left that part and settled in the shoulder,
et puis un poc aprés corrut par tout le cors, tant qu’ele vint en l’autre brais;	And then after a short while corrects throughout the body, until it reaches the other arm;
puis me contait qu’elle tornioit adés entor le cors, si com je la vis.	Then I realized that she was correcting internally within the body, as I observed.
Je me mervillai mout coment elle se movoit ensi de membre em membre, car je n’avoie onques veut ceste maladie selonc ceste maniere.	I marveled greatly at how she moved thus member by member, for I had never seen this disease in such a manner.
Toutevoie, je avoie veut maint que bien avoient veut movoir dolor de leu a autre,	Still, there have been many times when others have wanted to move pain from one part of the body to another,
mais je ne l’avoie mie veut, si com je le vis en la femme;	but I do not wish to use this method if it is as I see it applied on a woman;
et je me pensai que c’estoit por ceu que li femme avoit sec cors, et les voinnes descovertes,	and I thought that was why women have smooth skin and exposed veins,
et por ceu apparoit celle ventositez constrainte;	and this explains the constriction of wind (a medical term possibly referring to风气 or a particular condition) in them;
et n’aperent mie selonc ceste raison a ces qui sont delicious, et qui ont moistes cors et voinnes reponues.	yet they don't appear this way according to this reason for those who are healthy and have wet skin and covered veins.
Et quant tu vues curer ceste maladie, et li malaides sent celle dolor, s’elle t’apert si com nos avons dit,	And when you see this disease being cured, and the patient feels that pain, if it opens up as we said,
si la lie desus et desoz hastanment, et puis cope sus tant que cele ventositez constrainte au leu isse fuer;	if it extends upwards and downwards rapidly, and then apply it until the constraining windiness that comes out of the body occurs;
et cauterize le leu; et se tu ne la vois a tes eulz,	and apply cautery to this region; and if you don't see it in your eyes,
si le cure de ceu qui deboute les ventositez, si com pilules fetides, et pilules de serapin, et semblans autres.	if the treatment for those who expel wind includes things like stinking pills, and pills made from rattlesnake venom, or similar items.
Des saiettes	Of arrows
Les saiettes sont diverses, selonc lor semblances et selonc les leus dou cors ou elles chient.	Arrows vary, according to their appearances and according to the locations on the body where they pierce.
Li diversitez de lor si est qu’il i a de celles qui ont grans pointes, et petites, et chevees, et soudees;	The variety of their size includes those with large points, and small ones, and feathered ones, and soldered ones;
et de celles qui ont .ij. angles, et de celz qui ont lengues, et de celles ou il a pieces;	and there are those with two edges, and those with tongues, and those where they have parts;
et celle qui chiet en aucun membre si chiet selonc .ij. manieres: ou en membre principeil cheveit,	And when they give birth without any member, if it does so according to two ways: or among the main members, that one might have,
si com cerveil, cuer, foie, pormon, rains, intestine, vessie, et semblans membres.	such as brain, heart, liver, spleen, lungs, intestines, bladder, and similar organs.
Quant elle chiet donques en aucun leu de ces membres, et li signe de mort, que je te dirai ci aprés, t’aperent:	And when she gives birth then in no part of these members, and the signs of death, that I will tell you later, become evident:
si covient que tu te warses de l’estraction de ceste saiette, car li mors vient aprés en plusors dispositions;	it is necessary for you to be prepared for the extraction of this arrow, because death comes after in various situations;
et quant cist mal signe ne t’aperent mie, et li saiette n’est mie em parfont, si la trai, et cure la plaie.	And when you do not notice this symptom, and the arrow is not yet completely out, then pull it, and treat the wound.
Et li signe dou cerveil quant li saiette i chiet et perce l’os, et saut li syfac fuer qui est sus le cerveil,	And when the sign of the brain appears, as the arrow enters and pierces the bone, and sends a spasm upwards to the head,
est quant scotomie et sode et esvertin et roujor ens eulz, et enflammation et roujor de lengue, et spasme et permixtion d’entendement, et vomissemens de cole;	This is when blindness and numbness affect the tongue and body, and a red flush appears on their faces, along with inflammation and a red tongue, and seizures and confusion of mind, as well as vomiting of bile;
et per aventure ist sans fuer des narines, ou des oreilles; et par aventure pert la parole et la voix;	And it might affect the nose or ears too; and sometimes one loses speech and voice.
et saut de la plaie moistor blanche semblant a poulz, et en saut ausi com bruee de char;	And from the wound, there is moist white matter resembling hair, and also ash-like burnt flesh.
et se cist signe t’aperent, si te tien de la cure, et trai la saiette s’elle n’est ens.	And if you notice this sign, hold the treatment steady, and pull out the arrow if it hasn't been lodged.
Li signe de la siette quant elle chiet ou cuer, sont qu’elle est pres de la mamele senestre, et sent ausi com s’elle estoit fichie en chose dure, ne mie vuide;	The sign of the arrow when it hits or pierces is that it's near the left breast, and also as if it were stuck in something hard, not empty;
et par aventure li siette se muet ausi com li poulz, et en cort noir sanc, et vient froidor et suor froide, et sincope:	And by chance the arrow also moves like hair, and there is black blood, and coldness comes with cold sweat, and fainting:
saiches adonc sens doute ke li mors dessent.	Therefore, know that many die.
Et li signe de la saiette que nevre lou pormon est que sans plains d’escume saut de la plaie, et li gorge enfle, et li malaides mue color, et sospire haut et quiert le froit ar.
